				<script type="text/javascript">
			$J( function() {
				BindAutoFlyoutEvents();

				var $Window = $J(window);
				var $Header = $J('#store_header');
				var $ResponsiveNavWindowShadeCtn = $J('#responsive_store_nav_ctn');
				var $ResponsiveNavOverlay = $J('#responsive_store_nav_overlay');
				var $ResponsiveNavOverlayCtn = $J('#responsive_store_nav_overlay_ctn');
				var $ResponsiveNavOverlayBottom = $J('#responsive_store_nav_overlay_bottom');
				var $HeaderWrapper;
				$Window.on('Responsive_SmallScreenModeToggled.StoreMenu', function() {
					var bUseSmallScreenMode = window.UseSmallScreenMode && window.UseSmallScreenMode();

											if ( !$HeaderWrapper )
							$HeaderWrapper = $Header.wrap( $J('<div/>', {'class': 'responsive_store_nav_ctn_spacer'} ) ).parent();

						if ( bUseSmallScreenMode )
							$ResponsiveNavWindowShadeCtn.append( $Header );
						else
							$HeaderWrapper.append( $Header );


						if ( bUseSmallScreenMode )
						{
							$Header.css( 'visibility', 'hidden' );
							$Header.show();

							var nStartingScrollPosition = $J('#store_header').height();
							if ( $Window.scrollTop() < nStartingScrollPosition )
								$Window.scrollTop( nStartingScrollPosition );

							$Header.css('visibility', 'visible');
						}
									} );
				
				window.setTimeout( function() { $J(window).trigger('Responsive_SmallScreenModeToggled.StoreMenu'); }, 0 );

										var g_rgUserPreferences = {
							excluded_tags : [],
							excluded_content_descriptors : [3,4]						};
						
													g_rgUserPreferences['use_store_query'] = 1;
						
						g_rgUserPreferences['use_search_spellcheck'] = 1;
						g_rgUserPreferences['search_creators_and_tags'] = 1;

						if( $J('#searchform').length > 0 )
						{
							// default search support where the web page includes the search edit control
							EnableSearchSuggestions( $J('#searchform')[0].elements['term'], '1_5_9_', 'SG', 1, 'schinese', g_rgUserPreferences, '20235618' );
						}
						else 
						{
							// search support for the mobile client.  the mobile client has a native search edit control but relies on the web content to perform the query and show results
													}
				
				// make genre categories expand/collapse on mobile
				$J(document).on( 'click', '.popup_genre_expand_header', function ( event ) {
					if ( !UseSmallScreenMode() )
						return;

					event.preventDefault();
					var $Element = $J(this);
					var $Target = $J('.popup_genre_expand_content[data-genre-group=' + $Element.data('genre-group') + ']' );
					if ( $Element.data('group-expanded') )
					{
						$Target.slideUp();
						$Element.data( 'group-expanded', false );
					}
					else
					{
						$Target.slideDown();
						$Element.data( 'group-expanded', true );
					}
				});
			} );
		</script>

                                        <div class="slider" id="highlight_slider">

                                            </div>

                                            </div>

                                        <div id="highlight_slider_right" class="slider_right"><span></span></div>

                                    <script type="text/javascript">
                                        $J( function() {
                                            var player = new HighlightPlayer( {
                                                elemPlayerArea: 'highlight_player_area',
                                                elemStrip: 'highlight_strip',
                                                elemStripScroll: 'highlight_strip_scroll',
                                                elemSlider: 'highlight_slider',
                                                rgScreenshotURLs: rgScreenshotURLs
                                            } );

                                            $J('#highlight_slider_right').click( function() {
                                                player.Transition( true );
                                            });
                                            $J('#highlight_slider_left').click( function() {
                                                player.TransitionBack( true );
                                            });

                                            
                                                // swipe gesture handling for the media carousel

                                                // TODO: We may want to move all of this to the player class so it has built in touch gesture support.
                                                // First testing here as part of new mobile ux.

                                                var k_nElementWidth = 120;
                                                var k_playerItemClassName = '.highlight_player_item';
                                                var g_nStripWidth = 2520;
                                                var g_nMediaItems = player.m_elemPlayerArea.find( '.highlight_player_item' ).length;
                                                var g_TouchEventStart = null;

                                                // Handle left/right swipe on the media playback by moving forward or backward when the swipe completes
                                                $J('#highlight_player_area').on("touchstart", function (event) {
                                                    g_TouchEventStart = event;
                                                });
                                                $J('#highlight_player_area').on("touchmove", function (event) {

                                                    if ( typeof g_TouchEventStart == undefined )
                                                        return;

                                                    var xdiff = Math.abs( g_TouchEventStart.originalEvent.changedTouches[0].screenX - event.originalEvent.changedTouches[0].screenX );
                                                    var ydiff = Math.abs( g_TouchEventStart.originalEvent.changedTouches[0].screenY - event.originalEvent.changedTouches[0].screenY );

                                                    // To reduce unintended page scroll during a horizontal swipe block the default handler when it looks like the user
                                                    // is in the process of performaing a horizontal scroll
                                                    if ( xdiff > ydiff && ( typeof event.cancelable !== 'boolean' || event.cancelable ) )
                                                        event.preventDefault();

                                                });
                                                $J('#highlight_player_area').on("touchend", function (eventEnd) {

                                                    if ( typeof g_TouchEventStart.originalEvent.changedTouches[0] == undefined ||
                                                        typeof eventEnd.originalEvent.changedTouches[0] == undefined )
                                                        return;

                                                    var xdiff = g_TouchEventStart.originalEvent.changedTouches[0].screenX - eventEnd.originalEvent.changedTouches[0].screenX;
                                                    var ydiff = g_TouchEventStart.originalEvent.changedTouches[0].screenY - eventEnd.originalEvent.changedTouches[0].screenY;

                                                    // clear out the touch start event
                                                    g_TouchEventStart = null;

                                                    // ignore the swipe if it was short and could've been intended as a tap, or the
                                                    // direction was more vertical than horizontal
                                                    if ( Math.abs( xdiff ) < 20 || Math.abs( ydiff ) > Math.abs( xdiff ) )
                                                        return;

                                                    // we're handling this event
                                                    if ( typeof event.cancelable !== 'boolean' || event.cancelable )
                                                        event.preventDefault();

                                                    // move forward or backward but don't wrap as that would be a jarring user experience
                                                    if ( xdiff > 0 )
                                                    {
                                                        var $NextItem = player.m_activeItem.next( k_playerItemClassName );
                                                        if ( $NextItem.length )
                                                            player.Transition( true );
                                                    }
                                                    else
                                                    {
                                                        var $NextItem = player.m_activeItem.prev( k_playerItemClassName );
                                                        if ( $NextItem.length )
                                                            player.TransitionBack( true );
                                                    }
                                                });

                                                // when the thumbnail strip is swiped move the strip at a granular level
                                                // so it feels active.  The active image does not update because when testing the code to
                                                // make it change the active element it seemed annoying
                                                var g_nSwipeStartingPosition = 0;
                                                var g_nMaxScroll = g_nMediaItems > 3 ? ( ( g_nMediaItems - 3 ) * k_nElementWidth ) : 0;

                                                $J('#highlight_strip_scroll').on("touchstart", function (event) {
                                                    g_TouchEventStart = event;
                                                    g_nSwipeStartingPosition = parseInt( player.m_elemStripScroll.css( 'left' ) );

                                                    player.StopCycle();
                                                });
                                                $J('#highlight_strip_scroll').on("touchmove", function (event) {

                                                    if ( typeof g_TouchEventStart == undefined )
                                                        return;

                                                    // To reduce unintended page scroll during a horizontal swipe block the default handler when it looks like the user
                                                    // is in the process of performaing a horizontal scroll
                                                    var xdiff = parseInt( event.originalEvent.changedTouches[0].screenX - g_TouchEventStart.originalEvent.changedTouches[0].screenX );
                                                    var ydiff = parseInt( event.originalEvent.changedTouches[0].screenY - g_TouchEventStart.originalEvent.changedTouches[0].screenY );
                                                    if ( Math.abs(ydiff) > Math.abs(xdiff) )
                                                        return;

                                                    // move the scroll strip without changing the selected item
                                                    var nNewScrollPosition = parseInt( g_nSwipeStartingPosition + xdiff );

                                                    // check that we don't scroll past the ends
                                                    if ( nNewScrollPosition > 0 )
                                                        nNewScrollPosition = 0;
                                                    else if ( nNewScrollPosition < (-1 * g_nMaxScroll) )
                                                        nNewScrollPosition = (-1 * g_nMaxScroll);

                                                    // set the new scroll position
                                                    player.m_elemStripScroll.css( 'left', nNewScrollPosition + 'px' );

                                                    // we're handling this event
                                                    if ( typeof event.cancelable !== 'boolean' || event.cancelable )
                                                        event.preventDefault();
                                                });
                                                $J('#highlight_strip_scroll').on("touchend", function (eventEnd) {
                                                    g_TouchEventStart = null;
                                                    g_nSwipeStartingPosition = 0;
                                                });

										
                                            if( window.location.hash )
                                            {
                                                var ssid = window.location.hash.substr(1);
                                                player.HighlightScreenshot(ssid);
                                            }
                                        } );
                                    </script>
                                                            </div>
                        					</div>
				</div>
				<div style="clear: both;"></div>
			</div>
			</div>

						<div id="game_area_description" class="game_area_description">
							<h2>关于这款游戏</h2>
							<img src="https://cdn.akamai.steamstatic.com/steam/apps/722180/extras/description_image.png?t=1668208940"><br><br>Tired of all the wave VR zombie shooter games? Do you think what you have played so far is somehow too arcade?<br><br>Then forget what you have played so far, <strong>SURV1V3 is a unique realistic zombie survival fps game expressly designed for VR that will let you truly test your survival skills.</strong> Play the thrilling story in single mode or coop with your friends (up to 4 players) and survive the apocalypse!<h2 class="bb_tag"><strong>INFECTION DAY 407</strong></h2>It has been over a year since an unknown Seadornavirus released the V1V3 Virus. The first cases of the V1V3 Virus were report on the 14th November 2018, spreading it's deadly effects among world killing billions of people. Will humanity survive V1V3? Someone is supposing a cure can be found…<br><br>Fire, run, hide yourself, lockpick, pretend to be a zombie, be smart, plan your moves and coordinate with your teammates!<br><br>SURV1V3 is this and much more… starting from the infamous city of Santa Carla, narrow rotten sewers… endless creepy scenarios, scary situations and challenging tasks, until you meet the mysterious man who may be able to save the world.<br><br><img src="https://cdn.akamai.steamstatic.com/steam/apps/722180/extras/CoopTitles.gif?t=1668208940"><h2 class="bb_tag"><strong>FEATURES</strong></h2>How does it feel to fight side-by-side with someone, knowing that your life depends on him because you know you can’t do it alone? Will you be able to find your way knowing that the right one means salvation, while the wrong one means certain doom?<br><br>In SURV1V3 you will have a chance to face your answers, but you’re warned… Reality is damn scary!<br><br><strong>UP TO 4 ONLINE PLAYERS COOP</strong><br>Unexpected cooperative (up to 4 online players) and pervasive dynamics will take place when living the experience together with your friends, making the challenge even more exciting.<br><br><strong>HUGE FREE ROAMING MAPS</strong><br>Huge and fully explorable levels, including many buildings that are fully explorable to scavenging loot, pushing the player to a nonlinear approach to gameplay;<br><br><strong>3 GAME MODES</strong><br><ul class="bb_ul"><li>Story: more than 18 hours of gameplay to complete the thrilling story!<br></li><li>Trials: classic horde, defense mode, escape mode<br></li><li>Survival: leveling, crafting, feeding, fighting!</li></ul><br><strong>FULLY SIMULATED WEAPONS</strong><br>Rifles, machine guns, snipers, shotguns, handguns, bow: real bullet physics, reload gestures, realistic recoil &amp; bloom effects, manually attach and remove weapons accessories.<br><br><strong>IMMERSIVE REALISM</strong><br>No hud at all to be as immersive as possible, any option, dialogue, interaction menu is managed through a realistic military tablet.<br>Fully simulated player’s body, true life weapons reload, realistic zombie perception system, friendly fire.<br><br><img src="https://cdn.akamai.steamstatic.com/steam/apps/722180/extras/GameModeTitles.gif?t=1668208940"><h2 class="bb_tag"><strong>STORY</strong></h2>Your adventure begins after a car crash: the road is blocked, and you have to continue on foot… You can hear a message coming from the speakers from a distance, perhaps… could it be someone looking for help? Are you ready to save the world from the nightmare it plunged into?<br><br><br><strong>• DO THE RIGHT THING:</strong> A strange character guiding you through the radio seems to be your only hope for saving humanity. You just have to follow his advice and complete the tasks he’ll give you from time to time. 18 missions to face head-on, and tons of hours of gameplay to enjoy by yourself or with up to 3 friends!<br><br><strong>• EXPLORE:</strong> the town of Santa Carla, its complex sewer system, the industrial city of Portmain… the missions will take you through vast and freely explorable scenarios! Certainly getting around a zombie-infested world won’t be easy, and you’ll soon find that your trusty tablet and its highly detailed map can make the difference between life and certain death! In each mission you will also have secondary objectives, which will allow you to unlock accessories for your weapons or upgrades for your equipment.<br><br><img src="https://cdn.akamai.steamstatic.com/steam/apps/722180/extras/divisor2.png?t=1668208940"><h2 class="bb_tag"><strong>SURVIVAL</strong></h2>A whole city, thousands of zombies, only one shelter and other survivors like you in search of food and weapons. Humanity has sunk into its darkest moment, and the struggle for survival is getting harder day after day… never let your guard down! <br><br><br><strong>• LEVELING:</strong> Kill as many walkers as possible in order to gain experience points and increase your reputation. Each level you reach will unlock new rewards! <br><br><strong>• CRAFTING:</strong> you can craft new useful items for your survival by using the crafting machines that you will find around the city. By unlocking new blueprints, you will be able to create ever more powerful weapons and ammo!<br><br><strong>• LOOTING &amp; FEEDING:</strong> you will need water and food, new weapons and lots of ammo. It will also be important for you to collect materials and other items for making new ones! Always secure your loot in your home, and remember to close the front door properly! Another survivor could steal everything from you!<br><br><strong>• RANDOM EVENTS:</strong> not just survival… there’s always something to do in the city! Pay attention to the map on your tablet and test your skills, by always facing new random events which can even give you rare weapons and items!<br><br><img src="https://cdn.akamai.steamstatic.com/steam/apps/722180/extras/divisor.png?t=1668208940"><h2 class="bb_tag"><strong>TRIALS</strong></h2>Trials challenges are alternate missions requiring a particular skill and strategy to be completed successfully. Each test can be tackled individually or in cooperative mode. Whether alone or in company, your stamina skills will be tested! <br><br><br><strong>• LAST GARDEN:</strong> confined to the park of Santa Carla, hordes of walkers continue to advance with only one goal: eating fresh meat! Fight them with everything you’ve got and fend off 30 hordes, each one more deadly than the other… it won’t be easy, but you can do it! Or not?<br><br><strong>• HELL STREET:</strong> a sample of the V1V3 virus was lost along a walkers-infested street in Santa Carla, you have to recover it and wait for the helicopter to come and pick you up. you will find stations with weapons and ammo along the way, so play it well and maybe you can tell your grandchildren…<br><br><strong>• BIG BIRD:</strong> some antennas placed around the city are offline, fly aboard the helicopter from one antenna to another and activate them in sequence, while hanging on long enough to repel the hordes of zombies attracted by the noise. What could possibly go wrong?<br><br><br><img src="https://cdn.akamai.steamstatic.com/steam/apps/722180/extras/description_logo.png?t=1668208940"><h2 class="bb_tag"><strong>SURV1V3 IS DIFFERENT</strong></h2><ul class="bb_ul"><li>no hud at all to be as immersive as possible, any option/dialogue/interaction menu is managed through a realistic military tablet;<br></li><li>fully simulated weapons (e.g. bullet physics, reload gestures, recoil&amp;bloom effects);<br></li><li>manually attach/remove weapons accessories;<br></li><li>melee weapons;<br></li><li>friendly fire;<br></li><li>smart mechanics (e.g. disguise as a Zombie), pushing the player to a nonlinear approach to gameplay;<br></li><li>fully simulated player body;<br></li><li>+40 zombie models, with full dismemberment and realistic perception system (sight and sound);<br></li><li>huge and fully explorable levels (including many buildings that are fully explorable)<br></li><li>full locomotion (teleport is also supported);<br></li><li>up to 4 player cooperative story, trials and survival modes;<br></li><li>more than 18 (eighteen!) hours of gameplay in the thrilling story mode so far!</li></ul>						</div>

		<div class="leftcol">
							<div class="user_reviews_sub_header">最有价值的评测&nbsp;
					<span class="user_reviews_most_helpful_days">总体</span>
				</div>
				
	<div data-panel="{&quot;type&quot;:&quot;PanelGroup&quot;}" class="review_box    partial">
		<div id="ReviewContentsummary55517912">
			
			<div class="leftcol" id="ReviewContentsummary55517912_leftcol">
				<div class="avatar">
					<a href="https://steamcommunity.com/profiles/76561198163372466/">
						<div class="playerAvatar offline" data-miniprofile="203106738">
														<img src="https://avatars.akamai.steamstatic.com/7a419fe6e62bdb4fb343e2e7932e185e101264b9.jpg" srcset="https://avatars.akamai.steamstatic.com/7a419fe6e62bdb4fb343e2e7932e185e101264b9.jpg 1x, https://avatars.akamai.steamstatic.com/7a419fe6e62bdb4fb343e2e7932e185e101264b9_medium.jpg 2x">						</div>
					</a>
				</div>
				<div class="persona_name"><a href="https://steamcommunity.com/profiles/76561198163372466/" data-miniprofile="203106738">CrazyBus</a></div>
												<div class="num_reviews"><a href="https://steamcommunity.com/profiles/76561198163372466/recommended/">1 篇评测</a></div>
							</div>
			
			<div class="rightcol" id="ReviewContentsummary55517912_rightcol">
								<a href="https://steamcommunity.com/profiles/76561198163372466/recommended/722180/" class="vote_header tooltip" data-tooltip-text="阅读完整评测">
					<div class="thumb">
						<img id="votingImage" src="https://store.akamai.steamstatic.com/public/shared/images/userreviews/icon_thumbsUp_v6.png" width="40" height="40">
													<img class="responsive_voting_image" src="https://community.akamai.steamstatic.com/public/images/apphubs/bigpicture/thumbs_upselected.png" width="40" height="40">
											</div>

										<img class="review_source tooltip" data-tooltip-text="产品是从 Steam 直接购买的" src="https://store.akamai.steamstatic.com/public/shared/images/userreviews/icon_review_steam.png">
					
					<div class="title ellipsis">推荐</div>
										<div class="hours ellipsis">
						总时数 214.4 小时												（评测时 54.7 小时）											</div>
									</a>
				
									<div class="early_access_review tooltip" data-tooltip-text="该评测被撰写时，SURV1V3 被标记为 Steam 抢先体验游戏">抢先体验版本评测</div>
				
													<div class="responsive_review_leftcol_ctn" id="ReviewContentsummary55517912_leftcol_ctn"></div>
				
				<div class="postedDate">
					发布于：2019 年 10 月 9 日																					<div class="responsive_purchase_source">
															Steam 直接购买													</div>
									</div>

								
				<div class="content">
					截止到2019年10月18日，我在这款游戏上已经体验了将近100小时，故事模式已经全部通关，解锁了所有道具和皮肤，并且在新推出的生存模式当中积分排名前十。想交流的可以加qq3102883186<br><br>最早让我入坑丧尸游戏的是“亚历桑那阳光”，在困难模式下单人通关所有剧情和DLC以后被推荐了这款游戏。刚开始觉得上手困难，需要手动换弹夹以及拉枪栓，身上最多携带6个弹夹，不像“阳光”那样，手放到腰间就能自动上弹，能携带1300多发子弹。后来慢慢适应以后，就觉得这是一款非常棒的丧尸游戏。玩VR不就是追求沉浸感吗？在真实世界当中，枪就是得这么更换弹夹的，而且战斗时也不可能携带一千多发子弹，跑得动吗？所以，这款游戏更具有真实感和沉浸感。现在感觉已经回不去“阳光”了，因为“阳光”太小儿科，从头到尾拿枪突突，不够真实。<br><br>上个月，这款游戏开始支持中文字幕了，感觉我又可以再刷一遍故事模式，深入了解一下剧情，而不只是通关。另外，我还只是在茜茜（简单）和生存者（普通）两个难度下通关，还没有通关没有未来（困难）和噩梦（极困难）这两个更高难度，感觉前面路还很长。<br><br>当然，这款游戏也是有很多不足的地方，毕竟目前还只是“抢先体验版”。<br>首先是游戏玩家少，特别是中国玩家。我想可能是因为游戏的初始难度太大，造成新人容易放弃。如果能够降低游戏的初始难度，让新人更容易上手，相信会有更多玩家入坑的。比如，最开始的关卡应该是白天，让新手找到感觉；然后再到傍晚，最后才是深夜。而现在，第一关就直接是深夜，能见度很低，新手会因为害怕而放弃游戏，要让新手有兴趣玩足够长的时间，这样才能体验到这款游戏真正的魅力。<br>另外，建议对于新人要暂时关闭生存模式，必须通关故事模式才能开启。要不然，新人刚进游戏就玩生存模式，体验是极差的：所有武器配件都用不了，能见度低，僵尸又太凶。<br>另外，目前生存模式只能刷经验值和排行榜，显得有些单调，应该增加更多的任务和BOSS，这样趣味性就更强了。相信开发者们正在努力当中，很期待。<br><br>接下来，给新手玩家一些建议：<br>1.先玩故事模式，难度选“茜茜”（简单）。初始出门装备包括：背包放医疗喷剂和电钻；腰带放步枪弹夹和手枪弹夹各3个；手枪两把，分别放在左右大腿处；步枪一把放在胸口；手拿散弹枪。注意：步枪子弹和散弹枪子弹是不冲突的，可以同时放，这样能够增加整体子弹携带量。散弹枪子弹打完后，就直接把枪扔掉，改用步枪射击。<br>2.搜索每一关地图上的白圈，找到武器杂志，放进背包，就能解锁各种武器配件。我最常用的配件是：红外线和爆炸子弹（红色弹夹）。没有这些配件，后面的关卡很难通过，更不用说生存模式（难度更大）。<br>3.如果希望角色拥有不同的服装，就要记得搜索地图上的紫色小点，找到人物模型放进背包。每位角色除了初始服装以外，还有另外两套服装。我是后来才发现的，然后又刷了一遍故事模式，才找齐所有的服装。<br>4.如果觉得画面太黑看不清，可以在设置当中将亮度调成最大。<br>5.对于走动慢的僵尸尽量爆头，这样能够一枪解决，比较节省子弹。这也是为什么我喜欢用红外线的原因，爆头更方便。如果发现有僵尸从远处跑过来，先打断他的腿，腿的面积更宽，更容易打中，打中后他就只能趴在地上慢慢爬。跑动的僵尸想爆头会很困难，打身体只能让他暂时停顿，都不是很好的方法。<br><br>最后，给那些想体验生存模式的玩家分享一点经验：<br>1.生存模式类似于打怪升级的RPG游戏，经验和等级会不断积累，通过排行榜可以看到自己目前的排名。生存模式有白天和黑夜之分，大约是半小时白天，然后半小时黑夜，这样交替循环。<br>2.左手的显示器可以查看当前状态。右下角的4个图标分别是：饥饿、口渴、组队、出门，如果是红色就不好，会让经验积累变慢。左边的圆圈，蓝色的外圈是饥饿度，绿色的内圈是口渴度，尽量吃满，这样经验积累更快。圆圈中央会显示经验积累的倍数，如果显示是0就无法获得经验。所以正确的生存方式应该是：吃饱喝足并且尽量找人组队，这样经验积累和升级都是最快的。<br>3.注意在房间积累一些食物和水，发现食物和水，即使状态是满的不用吃，也要随手将食物和水拿起来丢在地上，这样过了一段时间后，在原来位置上又会刷新，而地上的也不会消失。从此，妈妈再也不用担心你不够吃喝了。<br>4.升级的好处是，背包能够携带更多物品，房间的箱子也能存放更多物品。初始背包是2空位，箱子是4空位，而现在我的背包有5个空位，箱子有7个空位。另外，还能够解锁一些新的装备，比如说：牛逼闪闪的蓝电刀和巨大的铲子，还有各种头盔，以及给武器和服装喷上不同的迷彩涂装。<br>5.在生存模式当中，随机会刷新BOSS，我曾经在两人组队的情况下，晚上遭遇了BOSS。两人均满装备的情况下都打不死BOSS，后来引到房间门口才打死。当然原因可能是我们没有一直爆头，大量的子弹都浪费在了BOSS的身体上。杀死BOSS以后会掉出一个牛皮纸头套。<br>6.如果是一个人玩生存模式，尽量慢慢走，不断清理远处的僵尸，不让僵尸有靠近自己的机会。能进房间就尽量进去，补充食物、水和弹药。<br><br>总的来说，我很喜欢这款游戏，感谢开发者的努力，希望能够持续更新，带给我们更多的惊喜。					<div class="gradient"></div>
				</div>

				<div class="posted">

				<div class="content">
					游戏是好游戏，丧尸末日题材里难得的VR精品了。就是有几点想要吐槽一下：<br>1.弓的操控做的稀烂，明明VR游戏射箭那么有趣，箭矢总拿不稳一跑就掉，放在弦上不想射了取消箭矢就会弄掉，手却黏在弦上……<br>2.箭袋只能塞进背包，取箭的操作繁琐。就不能连着箭袋挂背上腰上吗？那么多游戏都可以做到伸手摸箭速射了。<br>3.女性角色的主武器挂点只有胸前，每次收放一下主武器就得摸一下自己奶子，玩会游戏自己奶子都摸红了，强烈要求主武器可以挂肩上！					<div class="gradient"></div>

													<div class="responsive_review_leftcol_ctn" id="ReviewContentsummary94113004_leftcol_ctn"></div>
				
				<div class="postedDate">
					发布于：2021 年 6 月 21 日																					<div class="responsive_purchase_source">
															Steam 直接购买													</div>
									</div>

								
				<div class="content">
					-----------------------------------------------20210711-----------------------------------------------<br>花费26h 和朋友联机通关3难度剧情 最终BOSS打的痛不欲生(小怪无限刷实在太多了) 剧情相对老套(毕竟新的套路做出来符合口味也难)  一个人的时候真的不敢玩这游戏<br>-----------------------------------------------20210624-----------------------------------------------<br>目前存在一些莫名其妙的BUG，如：<br><br>1.oculus rifts设备可以直接绕过steamvr运行 但是退出游戏时无法完全退干净 会残留在后台需要任务管理器杀除<br><br>2.使用steamvr运行的时候 如果中途脱掉头显一段时间再次戴上 游戏会出现问题无法正常运行<br><br>操作方式(虽然有图但是有时候看图看不明白)：<br><br>左手摇杆移动 单独按下摇杆为蹲 按下方向时按下摇杆为跑<br><br>右手摇杆为转向<br><br>扳机键为开火/开门及其他互动<br><br>握持键为抓东西(按一下持续抓住,再按一下松开)<br><br>副手可以通过移动到配件/保险/枪栓并试用扳机键可以开关配件/切换开火模式/上膛<br><br>手枪可以挂在腰间两把  腰带可以放三个手枪弹匣 共计5*15发<br><br>主张武器可以挂在胸前 建议挂霰弹 弹药量7+30发<br><br>手上可以拿着步枪 腰带也能放三个步枪弹匣 一般为4*30发<br><br>道具栏可以存放：手电筒(完全没用) / 医疗喷雾 / 电钻(目前没见到有用 大部分安全屋门口基本都有) / 尸油 / 箭袋(限1 15发 可回收)<br><br>左右肩上可以挂近战武器/弓共计两把<br><br>弓想要背包抽箭 需要按住持弓手的扳机键 并将另一只手升到肩部按扳机键 即可拿去一只背包里的箭<br><br>配件可以手动安装 但是需要再每关的过程中拾取安装教程书(?)才可手动安装 再地图上白圈范围可以找到(如有多个白圈的话 仅有一个白圈有相关道具)<br><br><br>-----------------------------------------------20210621-----------------------------------------------<br>好JB酷炫					<div class="gradient"></div>
				</div>

													<div class="responsive_review_leftcol_ctn" id="ReviewContentsummary85188630_leftcol_ctn"></div>
				
				<div class="postedDate">
					发布于：2021 年 1 月 23 日																					<div class="responsive_purchase_source">
															Steam 直接购买													</div>
									</div>

								
				<div class="content">
					非常棒的一款游戏，作者很用心，值得推荐。目前硬要说缺点，生存模式地图就一张，生存模式储物箱空间太少导致收集乐趣全无。空投更新很棒，但毁于玩家储物箱太小。而且空投没食物！！<br>P.S:可以用手抓住僵尸的隐藏设定很有趣，希望可以完善这个抓握功能，顺便近战武器增加一些小刀之类的配合该功能，实现暗杀僵尸很不错！<br>A very good game, the author is very careful, it is worth recommending. At present, if you want to talk about the shortcomings, there is only one survival mode map, and the lack of storage space in the survival mode leads to no fun in collecting. The airdrop update is great, but the player’s storage box is too small. and the airdrop has no food!<br>P.S: The hidden setting that can catch zombies with your hands is very interesting. I hope this grip function can be improved. By the way, melee weapons are added with some small knives to cooperate with this function. It is very good to assassinate zombies!					<div class="gradient"></div>
				</div>
